<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыться.html>ры́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rýtʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порыться.html>поры́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыться.html>ры́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig <i>(in)</i></li>

<li>to rummage <i>(in)</i>, to ransack

***порядочный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>поря́дочный</a> (4415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porjádok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>поря́дочный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porjádošnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поря́дочнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поря́дочней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>decent, honest, respectable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> decent, sizable, considerable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> utter, out-and-out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>поря́дочный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подлец.html>подле́ц</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>porjádošnyj</b> podléc.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is an utter wretch.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" style="vertical-align:center;"><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посад.html>поса́д</a> (20463)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посад.html>поса́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посад.html>поса́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посад.html>поса́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посад.html>поса́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trading quarter <i>(situated outside city wall)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> suburb</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a> (1700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажать.html>сажа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to seat, to set</li>
<li>to plant</li>
<li>to put to jail</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́дка</a> (4295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posádka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>planting</li>
<li>embarkation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">trains<span class="ib-comma">,</span> airplanes</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boarding</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> landing</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetlétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посветлеть.html>посветле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvetlétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светлеть.html>светле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lighten, to become lighter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>после</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гроза.html>грозы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посветлеть.html>посветле́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posle grozy <b>posvetlélo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sky lightened after the storm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посветлеть.html>посветле́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vólosy u nevó <b>posvetléli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his hair became lighter in colour</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***посвистывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посвистывать.html>посви́стывать</a> (14230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистать.html>свиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвистывать.html>посви́стывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvístyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to whistle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шёл</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посвистывать.html>посви́стывая</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on šól <b>posvístyvaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he whistled as he walked</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***посвятить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвяти́ть</a> (2450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвяти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvjatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to devote, to dedicate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">various senses</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвяти́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стихи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдца</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>posvjatíl</b> éti stixí dáme sérdca.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He has dedicated these poems to his ladylove.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to initiate (into), to let (into)</li>
<li>to ordain (into), to consecrate (into)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвящённый</a> (2450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвящённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvjaščónnyj</span>)

***посвящаемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́емый</a> (10681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvjaščájemyj</span>)
</p>

***посвящать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́ть</a> (10681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвяти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posvjatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvjaščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвятить.html>посвяти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to devote, to dedicate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">various senses</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящать.html>посвяща́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стихи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдца</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>posvjaščájet</b> éti stixí dáme sérdca.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He dedicates these poems to his ladylove.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to initiate (into), to let (into)</li>
<li>to ordain (into), to consecrate (into)</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящение.html>посвяще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posvjaščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящение.html>посвяще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящение.html>посвяще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посвящение.html>посвяще́ний</a></b>)

***посев.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посев</a> (13302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посеять.html>посе́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poséjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but structurally as if from nonexistent imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*посева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*posevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare prefixed imperfectives in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, e.g. imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обсева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obsevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> to perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обсе́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obséjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">засева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zasevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> to perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:засеять.html>засе́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaséjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posév</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sowing</li>
<li>crops
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:площадь.html>пло́щадь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́вов</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plóščadʹ <b>posévov</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sown area; area under crops</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:посев.html>посе́вы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:всходить.html>всхо́дят</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>posévy</b> vsxódjat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crops are coming up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plating, seeding, inoculation</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поселить.html>посели́ть</a> (13097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сели́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">selítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поселить.html>посели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poselítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поселя́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle, to lodge</li>
<li>to inspire, to engender

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поселить.html>посели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poselítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
